E aprop entromet en la extremitat del nas una meca de drap de li, si la fractura es en una partida, o metz doas calguas, si la fractura es en doas partidas, e sia en la calgua grossitut de tanta quantitat que umpla le trauc del nas.
Insert a piece of linen cloth into the end of the nose if the fracture is in one part, or two tampons if the fracture is in two parts, and make the tampon thick enough to fill the nasal cavity.

E diysso alcus dels antics restauradors que las calguas sian enfundudas en boder, e sian permudadas en tot dia, mays no es vist a mi; habantz cove que la meca sia enfunduda en album de huou comfit am polvera de moli; e aprop layssa la qualgua entro que l’os sia fermat e sia endurazida la cartillage.
Some ancient restorers say that the tampons should be soaked in vinegar and changed daily, but I have not seen this; rather, the cloth should be soaked in egg white mixed with flour, and left in place until the bone is set and the cartilage hardens.

E alcunas veguadas sia entromes en le nas, en loc de calgua, pena de auca pus que es envolopada de drap de li leon; e sia que ja te la fractura del nas pus vehement e que le malaute no sia prohibit de inspiracio.
Sometimes, instead of a tampon, insert goose feather wrapped in linen, especially for more severe nose fractures, ensuring it does not obstruct the patient's breathing.

E aquesta causa no es a tu necessaria; e si voles, fay aquo, e si voles, fay calguas.
This is not necessary; if you prefer, use this method, or use tampons.

E si accideys autra veguada apostema caut, emplastra le nas am cerot o am coto enfus en vi agre e oli rozat, o am diaquilon.
If an abscess forms, plaster the nose with cerate or cotton soaked in vinegar and rose oil, or with diachylon.

Mays si no accideys apostema caut, lahoras cove que emplaustres aquel defora am farina de sizami e am polvera de enses cofitz am album de huou; e aprop pausa sobre lu stopa leon, e no lies le nas am alcuna causa.
If no abscess forms, apply a plaster externally with sesame flour and incense powder mixed with egg white; then place cotton over it, but do not bind the nose for any reason.

Mays si so trencats les osses del nas am fractura petita o so conminuitz, lahoras cove que scindas sobre aquels, e extraguas aquels am insturmentz que conveno ad aquels; e aprop cos la scissura, e cura aquela am aquo que encarna e consolida, e am emplastres ad aquo convenientz.
But if the nose bones are broken with a small fracture or are shattered, you must incise over them, extract them with appropriate instruments; then suture the incision, and treat it with substances that heal and solidify, and with suitable plasters.

E si accideys plagua dedintz le nas, lahoras cove que cures aquella am calguas e administra canulas de plom entro que sia de tot sanat.
If a wound forms inside the nose, treat it with tampons and insert lead canulas until it is completely healed.

Capitol .iiii.
Chapter 4:

De restauracio de la mandibula quan es trincada.
On the Restoration of the Jaw when it is Broken.

Quan la mandibula dejos es rompuda e la fractura de lu no es am plagua, reguarda lahoras si la fractura es deforas tant solament, e no es trencada en dos e es curvada a las partidas dedintz, lahoras la sua cognicio es leugiera.
When the lower jaw is broken without a wound, if the fracture is only external and not split into two, and is bent inward, it is easily recognized.

E cove donc, si la fractura es en la part dreyta, que tu intrometas le tieu indic senestre en la boca del malaute; e semblantment si la fractura es an la mandibula senestra, lahoras intromet le dit indic de la ma dreyta; e impelleys am aquel la gilbositat de la fractura dedintz am facilitat a las partidas defora, am la tua autra ma de la partida defora del os; am aquel decentment equa aquelam.
If the fracture is on the right side, insert your left index finger into the patient’s mouth; similarly, if the fracture is on the left side, insert your right index finger; push the bulge of the fracture inward easily to the outside with your other hand on the outside of the bone; gently align it.

E si la fractura de la mandibula ja es separada en doas, lahoras cove que administres extensio de doas partz segon rectitut entro que sia possibla la equacio de lu.
If the jaw fracture is already split into two, administer extension of both parts in a straight line until it is possible to align them.

E si accideys conmocio de dentz a disrupcio, lahoras strenh aquelas de las quals speras que romandran am fil de aur o de argent o de ceda; e aprop pausa sobre la mandibula trencada cerot, e aprop pausa sobre lu drap duplicat, e pausa sobre le drap gran stelha decentment fayta, o una pessa de sola engual a la longitut de la mandibula; e aprop lia aquela desus segon que a tu es apparelhada la liadura de lu e que conveneys la applicacio, entro que no es destruida.
If the teeth are dislocated or disrupted, tighten those you hope will stay in place with a thread of gold, silver, or silk; then place cerate over the broken jaw, then place a folded cloth, and over the cloth a large, properly made splint, or a piece of sole the length of the jaw; bind it appropriately so it stays secure.

E comanda al malaute que use de repaus e tranquilitat, e pausa la vianda de lu sorbicios leons.
Instruct the patient to rest and keep calm, and provide them with liquid food.

E si extimas que ja es alterada la figura en alcuna manieyra, lahoras tu te coyta e deslia aquel al tertz dia; e aprop rectifica aquo que ja es alterat de lu e emplaustra aquel am polvera de moli, am album de huou, o am farina de cisami, pus que tu auras ostat le cerot de lu, e pausa sobre le emplastra lana leon.
If you think the shape has altered in any way, untie it on the third day; then correct the alteration and apply plaster with flour, egg white, or sesame flour, after removing the cerate, and place cotton over the plaster.

E adonc cum sta annex e ajustat aquel emplastre sobre lu, e la disposicio del os no es alterada, layssa aquel, que no le deslies entro que sia sanat e strenh la fractura; quar motas veguadas aquesta fractura es streyta en tres sempmanas.
Once the plaster is set and the bone’s position is not altered, leave it in place until it is healed and the fracture is secured, which often happens within three weeks.

E si autra veguada accida apostema caut, lahoras administra aquo que havem dit motas veguadas en la sedacio de lu entro que sia sanat, e sia remaugut aquel apostema.
If another abscess forms, apply the same treatments we mentioned for healing until it is completely healed.

E si la fractura es am plagua, lahoras considera si es pessa del os separada o satagias, lahoras tu te subtilia que ostes aquelas satagias am aquo que conveneys ad aquo en la remocio de aquellas dels sturmentz.
If the fracture involves a wound, check if a piece of bone is separated or splintered, then delicately remove the splinters with appropriate instruments.

E si le orrifici de la plagua es streyt, lahoras tu le amplifique am le fleubotomi segon la quantitat de la tua necessitat.
If the wound opening is narrow, enlarge it with a phlebotomy instrument as needed.

E aprop quan tu auras ostat aquelas satagias, e de aquelas no sira remaugut re, lahoras tu cos le orrifici de la plagua si es ampla; e sino, pausa sobre aquela un dels emplaustres que conveneysso ad aquo e encarnan aquela, entro que sia sanada.
After removing the splinters, if nothing remains, suture the wound if it is wide; if not, apply a suitable plaster to heal it until it is fully healed.

Capitol .v.
Chapter 5:

De restauracio de la furcula quan es trinquada.
On the Restoration of the Collarbone when it is Broken.

Motas veguadas es trencada la furcula de la partida denant deves le muscle, e aquela fractura es fayta en una de tres manieyras.
Often the collarbone breaks in front near the muscle, and this fracture happens in one of three ways.

Quar o es trencada, o seperada, o es seperada en doas partz otra que no accidan satagias; e es leugier a la restauracio de lu; o es ayssi que accideysso en lu satagias, e es dificil a restauracio de lu; o es ayssi que la fractura es am plagua.
It can either be broken, separated, or split into two parts without splinters; this is easy to restore; or it can involve splinters, making restoration difficult; or it can be with a wound.

E la operacio en aquela, quan la fractura es ses plagua, es que tu fassas esser present dos ministres, per so que la un tengua le adjutori e siegua la furcula trencada, e l’autre extenda le col ves aquela partida.
In cases without a wound, have two assistants present, one to hold the assistant and the broken collarbone, and the other to extend the neck towards the fracture.

E aprop enguala la fractura am les tieus ditz entro que sia fayta la forma de lu segon que cove, e no sia en lu eminencia pauca ni concavitat.
Align the fracture with your fingers until it takes the proper shape, without any bulges or concavities.

E si indigeysses mes de extencio, lahoras cove que pauses dejos le titillic del malaute spera de drap o de lana, e sia la grandesa de lu segon la quantitat de la tua necessitat; e exten e eleva la furcula e coarta la spera am la tua ma entro que enguales la frectura segon que cove.
If more extension is needed, place a pad of cloth or wool under the patient's armpit, of appropriate size; extend and elevate the collarbone and compress the pad with your hand until the fracture is properly aligned.

E si no podes atirar la extremitat de la furcula a las partidas defora, per so quar es pervenguda al preon, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia ressupinat sobre la sua cervitz, e pauses sobre le muscle de lu un coyssi migier en grandeza.
If you cannot pull the collarbone outward because it is pressing against the skin, the patient should lie on their back, and you should place a small cushion under the muscle of the affected side.

E le ministre prema le muscle de lu a las partidas dejos entro que l’os de la furcula sia elevat que es en le preon en sus, e lahoras tu rectifique la fractura e enguala aquela am les tieus ditz.
The assistant should press the muscle downward until the collarbone is elevated from the skin, then you can correct and align the fracture with your fingers.

Mays si sentes satagias de la furcula e so maugudas, lahoras cove que fendes sobre aquela e extraguas aquelas satagias am facilitat.
But if you feel splinters from the collarbone and they are stuck, you must make an incision over it and easily remove the splinters.

E si es retenguda en le os, lahoras tu ingenia inscisio de lu am un dels inscissoris les quals has apparelhatz ad aquo, pus que havias pausat dejos la furcula le sturment que serve le ciphac; e es sturment de fust o de ferr del qual aquesta es la forma de lu:
If they are stuck in the bone, make an incision with one of the incising instruments you have prepared for this, after placing under the collarbone the instrument that serves the ciphac; it is a wooden or iron instrument shaped like this:

E es semblant a culier del qual aquesta es la concavitat; e sia la sua latitut segon aquo que has necessitat de lu, segon la grandeza del os o la pauqueza de lu.
It resembles a spoon with this concavity; its width should match your need, depending on the bone's size or narrowness.

Mays la longitut de lu sia segon que es a tu possible a la operacio; que haja doas extremitatz ayssi cum vezes, e la una extremitat sia ample e l’autre streyta.
Its length should be suitable for your operation, with two ends, one wide and the other narrow.

E si la disrupcio de la plagua la qual has inscidida quan has extraytas la satagia del os es ampla, e yest segur de apostema caut, lahoras tu ajusta las doas labias de la plagua am sutura.
If the incision made to remove the splinters is wide and you are sure of no pus forming, suture the wound's lips.

E si la disrupcio es pauca, o temes apostema caut, lahoras tu uemple la plagua am draps e pulvils segon la quantitat de la scissura de la plagua.
If the incision is small or you fear pus formation, fill the wound with cloth and powders as needed.

E si accideys apostema caut, lahoras infon drap en vi agre e oli rozat e vi, e pausa sobre aquel.
If an abscess forms, soak cloth in vinegar, rose oil, and wine, and place it on the wound.

Mays la strictura del os quan es ses plagua e ses seccio, es que pauses emplastre fayt de farina de moli am album de huou, e pausa sobre lu stopa leon, e aprop pausa la spera dejos le titillic de lu, si indigeyssas de aquela, e aprop pren humemate, so es torca la qual teno les Sarrazis, que sia mot longua, e sia latitut de lu de un palm o entorn aquel; e aprop pausa pulvils duplicatz sobre la stopa e l’emplastre; e aprop pren una stela de taula subtil de la qual la latitut d’ela sia de tres ditz e en longitut semblantment; e aprop envolopa aquela en drap, e aprop envolopa aquel drap am la stela en lo loc sobre le loc de la fractura; e aprop pausa humemati ayssi cum es revout, e revol aquela sobre le col de lu e dejos le titillic de lu sa e dejos le titillic de lu malaute, e reduseys aquela sobre tota partida, e quan vezes que la strictura de la fractura am strictura descent, e es aquo que no es occultat sobre tu.
However, the binding of the bone when it is without a wound or cut involves applying a plaster made of flour and egg white, covering it with cotton, and placing a pad under the patient's armpit if necessary. Then take a long cloth, like the one used by the Saracens, about a palm wide, and sprinkle doubled powders over the cotton and the plaster. Next, take a thin wooden splint about three fingers wide and of similar length, wrap it in cloth, and then wrap that cloth and splint around the area of the fracture. Bind it securely as described, wrapping it around the patient's neck and under the armpit of the healthy side and the injured side, covering the whole area. This way, the binding of the fracture remains firm and secure, which is not unknown to you.

E tot, que no sia mauguda la stelha desobre le os trencat; e per so cove que tu vejas le malaute quascun dia, que quan le liament es mollificat o vezas la stela ja esser remauguda, lahoras tu rectifica aquo e strenh la liadura.
Ensure the splint stays in place over the broken bone; check the patient daily, and if the binding loosens or the splint moves, correct and tighten it.

E aprop pausa le dormir del malaute sobre le col de lu, e pausa dejos le titillic de lu deves le dormir de lu en la nueyt un petit coyssi; per so que am aquel sia elevat le adjutori de lu del latz de aquel, e donc es elevada la la fractura de la furcula a elevacio del muscle; o sia le bras de lu liat al col de aquel.
When the patient sleeps, place a small pillow under their head to elevate the injured side, lifting the broken collarbone. Alternatively, tie their arm to their neck.

E no deslies le liament si no accideys en le loc prusiment o apostema, entro a xii dias.
Do not remove the binding unless there is swelling or an abscess, for twelve days.

E aprop renovelha le emplastre si has vista la facia de lu ad aquo, e ajusta en la strictura e restaura aquel e layssa entro que sia restaurat e sia coagulat la fractura de la furcula.
Renew the plaster if needed, adjust the binding, and leave it until the fracture is healed and solidified.

E es strenguda e comfortada segon le mes en xxviii dias, e alcunas veguadas en alcus homes es fayt en mens de temps de aquel.
The fracture usually stabilizes and strengthens within 28 days, though it can take less time in some people.

Capitol .vi.
Chapter 6: 

De restauracio de fractura de la spalla.
Restoration of a shoulder fracture.

Spatula tart es trencada en le loc lat de lu e no so trencatz de lu sino les marges.
The shoulder blade is broken in its central part and not in the margins but the edges.

E donc quan es trencat le loc de lu — e es trencat en le mieg loc de lu — e no es conogut sino per tocament, lahoras segon que es la figura de la fractura sforsa te la preparacio de lu e reduzir aquela segon la figura natural en tota manieyra de engen la qual es a tu possible.
So, when the fracture is in the middle of the blade and is only detectable by touch, you must prepare and reduce it according to the natural shape in every way possible.

E aprop pausa sobre le loc polvera de moli am album de huou e stopa leon; e aprop pausa pulvil de drap duplicat; e aprop pausa sobre lu stela lada de taula subtil segon la quantitat de la spatula tota o mays un pauc.
Then, place on the area powdered flour with egg white and wool; then place a folded cloth; and then place a thin wooden splint according to the size of the shoulder blade or slightly more.

Mays si dejos la stela es concavitat en alcu dels locs de la spatula, lahoras tu enguala aquela concavitat am stopa leon, e aprop pueja la stela segon equalitat.
But if there is a concavity under the splint in any part of the shoulder blade, then fill that concavity with wool and adjust the splint accordingly.

E aprop strenh desus am humemati longua ab constriccio decent e am fermesa de la stela entro que no sia remauguda del sieu loc.
Then tighten with a long bandage with appropriate constriction and firmness of the splint so it does not move from its place.

E considera le liament en quascun dia; e totas veguadas que sia mollificat, lia autra veguada e stren le e equa la stela si es remauguda del sieu loc.
Check the bandaging every day; whenever it becomes loose, re-bandage and tighten it and adjust the splint if it has moved.

E jagua le malaute sobre le sieu latz sa.
Make the patient lie on their healthy side.

E la spatula es restaurada en xx dias o en .xxv.
The shoulder blade will be restored in 20 or 25 days.

E donc quan es complit aquest nombre, lahoras tu dissolveys le liament, e que tu scias ensegurat quar aquela es dels osses dels quals la cominicio no es temuda ni lor dissolucio.
When this time is completed, then remove the bandaging, knowing that the shoulder blade is one of those bones whose healing is not feared nor its dissolution.

E si procezeys del loc del os pessa e pongeys dejos la codena, lahoras tu scindeys sobre lu, e osta le, e fay segon que havem dit en la fractura de la furcula de sadacio de apostema caut si accideys aqui.
And if any piece of bone protrudes and pricks under the skin, then cut over it, remove it, and treat as we have mentioned in the fracture of the collarbone if this condition occurs.

Capitol .vii.
Chapter 7: 
De restauracio de la fractura del pietz.
Restoration of a chest fracture.

Le pietz alcunas veguadas es romput en le mieg loc de lu e aquo tart endeve; mays las extremitatz de lu mot endeve que so ciccadas e comminuidas.
The chest sometimes breaks in the middle and this often happens; but its edges are very often crushed and fragmented.

E dels accidentz de lu quan es trencat le mieg de lu es que declina a las partidas dedintz e accideys a lu gran dolor, e dificultat en lo hale, e tos, e fort leu e vomeys sanc; e es declarada en lu cavitat en le os trencat e no es occulta al sentiment.
And one of the accidents of a middle fracture is that it leans inward, causing great pain, difficulty in breathing, coughing, and often spitting blood; this is evident in the cavity of the broken bone and is not hidden from feeling.

E la restauracio de lu es que sia resupinat le malaute sobre le sieu dos, e pausa entre las spallas de lu un coyssi; e aprop prem als muscles de lu, e ajusta las costas de lu am las mas de dos costatz, e subtilia te en la operacio de lu e en la equacio segon tota manieyra que es ad aquo possibla e que conveneys ad aquo, entro que retorne la figura del os segon que cove.
The restoration involves having the patient lie on their back and placing a cushion between their shoulders; then press the muscles, adjust the ribs with hands on both sides, and work gently in the operation and alignment in every possible way until the bone's shape is restored.

E aprop pausa sobre lu emplastre e estopa e pausa desobre astela de taula subtil de sauze o de caligi e de a lor semblantz en levitat, pus que tu envolopas aquela en drap; e aprop subtilia te en lian aquela sobre le os trencat que no sia maugut; e vay am liadura segon retonditat al dors alcunas veguadas, e strenh aquel am strictura decent; e aprop considera la liadura en tota hora, e quan es mollificada strenh aquela.
Then place a plaster and wool on it, followed by a thin wooden splint made of willow or similar light wood, wrapped in cloth; gently bandage it over the broken bone so it does not move; wrap it round the back several times, and tighten it decently; check the bandage regularly and tighten it when it loosens.

E si necessitat provoca a desliament de aquela deves corrossio o pruziment, o dolor, o apostema que accideysso en le loc, lahoras tu coyta e deslia aquella e erradica le emplastre e rectifique aquo que accideys per aquo am manieyra de curacio de lu; e aprop reduzeys le emplastre, si vezes ad aquo la facia; e ajusta a lu strictura entro que sia sanat.
If a need arises to remove the bandage due to erosion, itching, pain, or abscess, quickly remove it, clean the plaster, rectify the situation with appropriate treatment, and then replace the plaster and tighten it until it heals.

Capitol .viii.
Chapter 8:
De restauracio de las costas quan son trincadas.
Restoration of fractured ribs.

Sapias que fractura de las costas no catz sino en locs grosses que siegon le dos; e de las extremitatz de lor de la partida denant no accideys ad aquellas contricio sino per aquo quar so cartillaginosas.
Know that rib fractures occur only in thick parts near the back; fractures in the front do not happen because they are cartilaginous.

E cognicio de lu no es amaguada al sentiment deves la inquisicio de lu am les ditz.
Detection of a fracture is not hidden from touch with fingers.

E la restauracio sia ayssi que enguales la fractura am les ditz segon la manieyra possibla, entro que sia engulhat segon que cove, e aprop emplastre e strenh le os trencat am stela, si indigeys de aquel.
Restoration involves aligning the fracture with fingers as much as possible until it is set, then plastering and tightening the broken bone with a splint, if needed.

E si la fractura de las costas es declinant a las partidas dedintz, lahoras accideys al malaute dolor vehement e punctura, ayssi cum punctura que accideys ad aquel que ha pleureci, e per aquo quar le os ponh le velament; e accideys a lu difficultat de hanelit, e tos, e vomit de mot sanc; e aquesta es de dificil curacio.
If the rib fracture leans inward, the patient will have severe pain and puncture similar to pleurisy, because the bone pricks the membrane; causing difficulty breathing, coughing, and often spitting blood; this is hard to cure.

E ja les Antixs so engeniatz en aquela am motz engientz.
The Ancients have worked on this with many inventions.

E de lor so que diso: cove que pauses viandas del malaute que engendro imflacio e ventositat, per que le ventre sia imflat e sia extendut, e la fractura sia impellida a las partidas defora.
Some said the patient should eat foods that cause bloating and gas, so the abdomen swells and the fracture is pushed outward.

Mays nos avoreyssem aquo per so que no sia causa leugiera a generar apostema caut, si no accideys; e si ja accideys, lahoras ja ajuda ad aquo.
But we avoid this as it may cause an abscess, and if it happens, it is helpful.

E diyssero alcus de lor que sia pausada desus ventoza e aprop que sucque am fortitut; e es semblant a ratiocinacio, mays empero es temut que la ventoza atire las superfluitatz al loc per la debilitat.
Some said to use a cupping glass to suck forcefully; this seems reasonable but feared to draw impurities to the area due to weakness.

E diyssero alcus de lor: cove que·l loc sia cubert am lana que ja es submersa en oli caut, e sian pausatz pulvils entre las costas entro que sia umplida, que sia la liadura engual quan envolopas aquela segon retonditat; e aprop sia curat le malaute am curacio de pleuresi de vianda e de medicina.
Some said the area should be covered with wool soaked in hot oil, with padding between the ribs to fill it, wrapped with bandages in a rounded manner; and the patient should be treated as for pleurisy with diet and medicine.

E si causa vehement constrenh le malaute la qual no sufferta, e le os punh le velament am punctura ledent, temem sobre le malaute, lahoras cove que fendam sobre le loc, descubram de la costa trencada, e aprop pausem desobre aquela instrument que conserve le ciphac, la rememoracio del qual es precedida, e que inscidam le os am facilitat, e extraguam aquel.
If severe pain constrains the patient, with the bone puncturing the membrane and causing distress, cut over the area, expose the broken rib, use the instrument to hold the diaphragm (mentioned earlier), cut the bone, and extract it.

E aprop que ajustem las doas labias de la plagua, si es gran, am cozidura, e curem aquela am emplastres entro que sia sanada.
Then align the wound edges if large, with stitching, and treat with plasters until healed.

E si accideys dedintz apostema, lahoras tu coyta e enfon pulvils en oli rozat e pausa sobre le loc, e que sia curat le malaute am aquo que cove a la apostema dedintz.
If an internal abscess occurs, quickly apply soaked pads in rose oil to the area, and treat the patient appropriately for the internal abscess.

E sia ressupinat sobre le latz sobre le qual dorm, entro que sia sanat.
Have the patient lie on the side they usually sleep on until healed.

Capitol .ix.
Chapter 9:
De restauracio de fractura del spondil del dos e del col.
Restoration of spinal fractures and neck bones.

Alcunas veguadas endeve fractura als osses del col, e tart endeve a lor atricio, e semblantment als spondils del dos.
Sometimes the bones of the neck fracture, often by pressure, and similarly with the spine.

E cum aquo accideys ad alcu e voles saber si sara sanat o no, lahoras considera, quar si vezes las sieuas mas ja mollificadas e stupefaytas e mortas e no pot maure aquelas ni extendre ni strenher aquellas e quan constrenges aquelas am les tieus ditz o punges aquellas am agulha e no sent en aquellas dolor, lahoras sapias que no es sanat, e en las mes de disposicios es mortal.
When this happens, and you want to know if it will heal, consider: if the patient's hands are softened, stupefied, and lifeless, unable to move, extend, or grip, and when you press or prick with a needle, there is no pain, then know it will not heal, and this condition is mostly fatal.

E si mau aquelas e sent en aquelas constriccio am les ditz e punctura, lahoras sapias que la nucha de l’os es salva e que le malaute guereys am curacio.
If there is movement and sensation when pressed or pricked, then know the spinal cord is intact, and the patient will recover with treatment.

E si ve als spondils del col le semblant ad aquo e voles saber si sira sanat o no, lahoras considera als pes de lu.
If the same occurs with neck vertebrae, and you want to know if it will heal, examine the patient's feet.

Lahoras si tu vezes que so ja mollificatz, accideys ad aquels aquo que es accidit en las mas, e aprop quan jatz sobre le sieu dos, yeys ventozitat e egestio ses la sua volontat, e alcunas veguadas es resupinat sobre le sieu dos e vol urinar e no pot, lahoras sapias que es mortal, e adonc no trebales en la curacio de lu.
If the feet are softened and experience the same as the hands, and when lying on their back, the patient passes gas and stool involuntarily, or if they try to urinate and cannot, know it is fatal, and do not attempt treatment.

Mays si no accideys alcuna causa de aquelas, la causa es milhor e pus leugiera.
If none of these conditions occur, the prognosis is better and easier.

E la curacio de lu es que te perforses a la sedacio del apostema caut que pauses sobre le spondil atrissat oli rozat sol, o am mugols de huous asatz; pausa sobre aquela aquel alcunas veguadas le dia entro que sia sedat le apostema caut.
The treatment involves sedating the inflamed area by applying rose oil alone or with yolks of roasted eggs several times a day until the inflammation subsides.

E lahoras pausa un dels emplastres confortantz e exsitans, e strenh sobre aquel am liament; e comanda al malaute que use de repaus e de tranquillitat e que no dorme sobre la partida am la qual atroba dolor entro que sia sanat.
Then apply one of the comforting and stimulating plasters, bandage tightly, and advise the patient to rest and avoid lying on the painful side until healed.

E si accideys deves la atricio del os satagias o alcuna causa que ja es seperada de lu, lahoras cove que secces sobre la codena e que ostes aquel os; e aprop ajusta las doas labias de la plagua, am sutura si es gran; e aprop cura aquela am alcu encarnatiu dels enguentz, entro que sia sanat.
If a bone fragment or cause is separated from the pressure, cut over the area and remove the bone; align the wound edges with stitching if large; then treat with healing ointments until healed.

Mays si es trencat le derier del os alhoses, e es la fi de la coeta, lahoras cove que tu entrometas le dit pous de la ma senestra en le cul, e que enguales le os trencat am l’autra ma segon que es possible per equacio segonda; e aprop pausa sobre lu emplastre e astelha, si indigeysses de aquels, e aprop strenh aquel.
If the last vertebra is broken and at the end of the tailbone, insert the thumb of your left hand into the anus, and align the broken bone with the other hand as possible; then apply plaster and splint if needed, and tighten.

E si sentes satagias trencadas en lu, lahoras tu fen sobre aquela, e osta aquel, e cura la plagua am la curacio que es precedida entro que sia sanada.
If you feel broken fragments, cut over them, remove, and treat the wound as previously described until healed.

Capitol .x.
Chapter 10: 
De restauracio de la ancha.
Restoration of hip fractures.

Les osses de las anchas tart so trencats, e si trencan, lahoras la fractura de lor no es sino communicio en las extremitatz de aquelas e son inscidas en la longitut e declinan a las partidas dedintz; e accideys al malaute dolor en le loc e punctura, e la camba es stupefacta quan es fractura.
The hip bones rarely break, but when they do, the fracture is usually at the ends, extending lengthwise and inclining inward, causing pain and puncture in the area, and the leg becomes stupefied.

E la restauracio de lu es que tu extendas la tua ma sobre aquel entro que sia sobre la fractura qual es la figura de lu.
The restoration involves extending your hand over the fracture to align it as it should be.

E si fractura es en la extremitat de lu tant solament, lahoras tu enguala aquela segon que a tu es apparelhat per equacio engual entro que sia asemblat a la sua figura natural.
If the fracture is only at the end, align it as much as possible until it resembles its natural shape.

Mays si la fractura es en le lonc o que ja declina a las partidas dejos, lahoras tu fay jaser le malaute sobre le sieu ventre entro que sia preparada a tu la restauracio de aquela fractura.
If the fracture extends lengthwise or inclines downward, have the patient lie on their belly until the fracture is prepared for restoration.

E donc quan auras engualada aquela, pausa sobre lu emplastre, e aprop pausa sobre aquel astela de fust o de codena, e strenh per strictura sobre la qual no temas punctacio de fractura ni remocio de la stelha.
Once aligned, apply plaster, then a wooden or leather splint, and tighten without fearing fracture puncture or splint movement.

E enguala la concavitat am aquo que uempla aquela entro que aquela prengua la strictura segon equalitat, e comanda al malaute que dorma sobre le sieu dos o desobre le sieu costat sa.
Fill any concavity to maintain even pressure, and advise the patient to sleep on their back or healthy side.

Mays si accideys apostema caut, lahoras tu cessa de extencio de lu e de la sua restauracio entro que sia sedat le apostema caut, e pausa sobre lu aquo que sede aquel segon que es precedit; e aprop retorna a la restauracio de lu, e strenh aquel ayssi cum cove.
If an abscess occurs, stop extending and restoring until the abscess subsides; apply treatments to sedate it, then resume restoration and tighten as needed.

E si accideysso en le os satagias o son comminuidas, lahoras tu las tratz.
If bone fragments are present or comminuted, remove them.

Capitol .xi.
Chapter 11: 
De restauracio de la fractura del adjutori.
Restoration of fractures of the elbow.

Adjutori es aquo que es entre le coyde entro al cap de la spalla.
The elbow is what is between the elbow joint and the shoulder.

E si es trencat, lahoras la restauracio de lu es en una de doas manieyras, de las quals es la una que tu prenguas fust pla de migiera groceza segon aquesta forma:
If it is broken, the restoration is done in one of two ways, the first being to take a flat piece of wood of moderate thickness shaped like this:

E sian liatz en doas extremitatz dos liamentz, e aprop sia suspendut del loc elevat.
Tie two bandages at both ends and suspend it from a high place.

E segua le malaute sobre una sezela; e aprop gieta fora le sieu bras trencat sobre le fust entro que pervengua al titillic de lu en le mieg loc del qual sia annexa la curvitat del fust.
Have the patient sit on a chair and extend the broken arm over the wood until it reaches the middle, where the curvature of the wood attaches.

E aprop suspen sobre aquel alcuna causa greu, o·l minestre extenda aquel a las partidas dejos; e aprop le metge eque la fractura am las sieuas mas ensemps, entro que la fractura retorne segon que cove.
Then suspend a heavy object from it, or have an assistant extend it downward; the doctor aligns the fracture with their hands until the fracture returns to its proper position.

E l’autra manieyra es que·l malaute sia ressupinat sobre la sieua cervitz e suspen la ma del col de lu am liament; e aprop comanda a dos ministres que la un de lor tengua aquo que es desobre la fractura am las suas mas; e l’autre tengua le pus dejos de lu; e quascu de lor extenda a la sua partida.
The other method involves the patient lying on their back, with the hand suspended by a bandage from the neck; instruct two assistants to hold above and below the fracture, each extending in their direction.

E si voles que la extencio sia pus fort, lahoras tu strenh sobre la fractura am liament e sobre aquela am autre liament, e quascu dels dos ministres extendan a doas suas partidas.
If you want stronger extension, tighten the bandage over the fracture with another bandage, and have each assistant extend in their direction.

E donc si la fractura es propinquada a la extremitat del muscle, lahoras cove que sia pausat la mitat del liament sobre le citillic e l’autre dejos la fractura deves le coyde.
If the fracture is near the end of the muscle, place half the bandage over the shoulder and the other below the fracture towards the elbow.

E semblantment si la fractura es propdana al coyde, lahoras cove que sia pausat le liament sobre aquel loc e sobre aquel coyde.
Similarly, if the fracture is near the elbow, place the bandage over that area and the elbow.

Enguala aquela am facilitat e ses trebal, e aprop quant sira engualada segon que cove e es applicada per bona applicacio, lahoras strenh aquela si no accideys apostema caut.
Align it easily without effort, and once properly aligned and applied, tighten unless an abscess occurs.

Mays si accideys apostema caut, lahoras layssa la strictura entro al vii dia, e pausa sobre lu lana sutza enbeguda en vi agre e oli rozat entro que repause le apostema, e lahoras tu stren aquela.
If an abscess occurs, leave the tightness until the seventh day, then apply dirty wool soaked in vinegar and rose oil until the abscess subsides, then tighten again.

E la manieyra de strenher aquela es que pauses emplastre sobre la fractura, e aprop pausa envolopament de drap nau sobre le emplastre; e aprop ajuste le bras sobre aquel adjutori, e pause la sua ma uberta sobre le sieu muscle.
To tighten, apply plaster over the fracture, wrap it with a clean cloth, adjust the arm over the elbow, and place the hand open on the muscle.

E pausa le drap e strenh sobre le adjutori le bras per so que·l bras sia en loc de stelhas, si no prohibeys de aquo alcuna causa del os trencat.
Wrap and tighten the cloth around the elbow so that the arm acts as a splint, unless prevented by a broken bone.

E lahoras usa de stelhas.
Then use splints.

E es que pauses sobre la fractura aquela stela que sia pus lada e pus fort de las autras stelas; e pausa entre quascuna stela la latitut del dit, e sia la longitut de las stelas segon la trencadura am addicio de tres ditz de tota partida.
Place the widest and strongest splint over the fracture, with the width of a finger between each splint, and the length of the splints extending three fingers beyond the fracture.

E aprop strenh sobre las stelas am la strictura la qual he dita al comensament del capitol.
Tighten the splints with the bandage as described at the beginning of the chapter.

E es que la tua strictura sobre le loc de la fractura sia pus streyt.
Ensure the bandage over the fracture is the tightest.

E quant pus es alonguada la fractura sia la strictura menor.
The longer the fracture, the looser the bandage should be.

E donc si vezes le situament de las stelas e la strictura ayssi cum havem dit en la hora en la qual restauras le membre al sieu assituament, lahoras tu fay.
When positioning the splints and bandages as described, restore the limb to its proper alignment.

E si temes apostema caut, lahoras tu layssa la strictura e las stelas entro al dia vii ayssi cum havem dit.
If you fear an abscess, leave the bandage and splints in place until the seventh day as described.

E aprop considera le liament en totas partidas per tres dias per so que no accida en le loc pruziment o imflacio; o es prohibida la vianda pervenir al membre per disposicio de superfluitat de strictura; e donc rectifiqua tot aquo segon que havem dit.
Check the bandage in all areas for three days to prevent itching or swelling, or the restriction of food to the limb due to excessive tightness; then adjust as needed.

Mays si tu yest sobre confizanssa que no accida alcuna causa de aquo, lahoras no deslias la liguadura sino aprop tres dias o mays.
If confident that none of these issues occur, do not loosen the bandage for about three days or more.

E sia la sua dormicio del malaute sobre le sieu dos, e las sieuas mas sian sobre le stomac.
Have the patient sleep on their back with their hands on their stomach.

E pausa sobre le adjutori cocena plena de lana engualment, e considera en tota hora de la nueyt o del dia que no sia deliada ni dissolta la figura del membre trencat, o que sia le liament mollificat, donc rectifica aquo tot am la tua vertut.
Place a wool-filled cushion evenly on the elbow, and regularly check that the limb's alignment and bandage are intact; adjust if necessary.

E pausa la vianda del malaute segon le orde le qual havem denant mes, enayssi que la vianda sia subtil en le comensament entro que es comensat strenher; e lahoras cove que egrossas la vianda de lu.
Feed the patient according to the prescribed order, starting with light food until tightening begins; then increase the food's substance.

Quar de constuma del adjutori e de la camba de lu es que sian strengutz en xl dias; e lahoras cove que sian desliatz e sia administrat banh e sia medicat am enguentz los quals rectifican aquel.
The usual treatment for the elbow and leg takes forty days; then loosen, bathe, and apply ointments to heal.

E si la fractura es layha atrita, lahoras tu no deslies de aquela le liament e las stelhas entro a l dias o entro a dos meses.
If the fracture is severe, do not loosen the bandage and splints for thirty to sixty days.

Capitol .xii.
Chapter 12: 
De restauracio de fractura del bras.
Restoration of fractures of the arm.

Bras es compost de dos osses les quals so appelatz dos focils; dels quals la un es petit, e es aquel que siec le dit pous, e l’autre es gran e es aquel le qual es pausat dejos le petit dit, de la partida pus dejus.
The arm consists of two bones called the forearm bones; one is small, located near the thumb, and the other is larger, located near the little finger, on the lower side.

E fort leu es trencat le focil major solament, o le petit, e fort leu son trincatz ensemps.
The larger bone often breaks alone or with the smaller bone.

E quan es trencat le focil petit desus, lahoras la restauracio de lu es leugiera, e la sanacio de lu es pus leugiera.
When the small upper bone breaks, the restoration and healing are easier.

E quan es trencat le focil de lu dejos la fractura de lu es mala, e la sanacio de lu es dificil.
When the lower bone breaks, the fracture and healing are more difficult.

E pus mala de aquela es quan son trencatz dos osses essemps.
The worst case is when both bones break together.

Donc si l’os le qual es trencat es le focil petit desus, lahoras es convenient al metge, deves la restauracio de lu, que pauze petita extencio am facilitat entro que aquel sia engualhat.
If the small upper bone breaks, it is advisable for the doctor to apply gentle extension until it is aligned.

Mays si le focil gran es aquo que es trincat, lahoras cove que pause extencio pus vehement.
If the larger bone breaks, a stronger extension is needed.

E si les dos focils so ensemps trincatz, lahoras cove que tu pauses la extritura mot pus fort.
If both bones break together, apply a much stronger extension.

E cove que pauses la figura de la ma deves la restauracio de lu e la extencio de lu estenduda sobre un coyssi, e sia le pols de la ma a las partidas desus, pus aut que totz les autres ditz, e le dit auricular sia pus bas dels autres ditz, e le malaute sia cezent sobre una cezela cayrada.
The hand should be positioned with the thumb higher than the other fingers, resting on a cushion, and the patient sitting on a square seat.

E sia un coyssi denant lu en la altetut o endreyt de lu, per so que·l malaute no encorra trebalh.
Place a cushion in front at the appropriate height to avoid discomfort.

E aprop le ministre extenda le bras de la partida pus dejos am la sieua ma o am liament, e autre ministre extenda desus semblantment.
One assistant extends the lower part of the arm with their hand or a bandage, while another does the same for the upper part.

E aprop le metge engualhe le os entro que redugua aquel segon la milhor figura que pot.
The doctor aligns the bone to restore it to the best possible position.

E si en la factura del os so satagias, lahoras te perforsa raduzir tota pessa en le sieu loc am la tua vertut.
If there are bone fragments, you must place each piece in its proper location with your skill.

E si appar en lu satagia separada que punh la codena e no es a tu speransa en la restauracio de lu, lahoras tu fen sobre lu e osta aquela segon la manieyra la qual havem dita desus.
If a fragment appears separated and pierces the skin without hope of restoration, treat it as previously described.

Mays si la fractura es am plagua, yeu ja he fayt ad aquo capitol singular, e donc pren la curacio de aquel.
If the fracture involves a wound, refer to the specific chapter on this and follow its treatment.

E si accideys apostema caut al comensament de la tua restauracio, lahoras tu lineys un drap am cerot fayt de oli rozat e cera blanca, e sia migier entre specitut e subtilitat, e strenh drap sobre aquel am strictura subtil entro que le apostema sia cedat; e lahoras remau le cerot e pausa emplastre preparat de polvera de moli am clayre de huou, e aprop pausa stelhas; e sia la stela la qual es pauzada sobre aquela fractura pus lada e pus fort.
If an abscess occurs at the beginning of the restoration, apply a cloth with cerate made of rose oil and white wax, moderately thick, and tighten it gently until the abscess subsides; then remove the cerate, apply a plaster made of powdered herbs and egg white, and use the widest and strongest splint over the fracture.

E sapias que·l nombre de las stelas del bras so vi en las majors disposicios, o sia la fractura en un focil o en dos focils ensemps.
Know that the number of splints for the arm is six in major cases, whether one or both bones are fractured.

E aprop pausa la tua strictura sobre le loc de la fractura pus fort e pus vehement, e quan mays sira la extrictura a las partidas desus de la fractura o a las partidas pus bassas de lu, pausa la strictura un pauc pus molh segon que es precedida la rememoracio de lu en le comensament del capitol.
Then apply the bandage most tightly over the fracture, loosening it slightly above and below as mentioned earlier.

E les draps que so envolopatz sobre la fractura sian draps mols humitz, e no sian durs ni aspres, e·l fiel am le qual es strenhut sia de li propriament migier entre subtil e gros, ayssi cum havem recomtat.
The cloths wrapped around the fracture should be soft and damp, not hard or rough, and the string used for tightening should be moderately thick, as described.

E considera le membre e·l liament aprop alcus dias.
Check the limb and bandage regularly for a few days.

E si accideys alcuna causa de la qual rectificacio es necessaria, ayssi cum prusiment le qual accideys al membre, e lahoras cove que tu enbroques le membre am aygua cauda entro que cesse aquel pruziment.
If an issue requiring correction arises, such as itching, soak the limb in warm water until it subsides.

E leysses le membre no costreyt entro que repause, e aprop torna la strictura.
Leave the limb untightened until it rests, then reapply the bandage.

E si la extrictura ja es mollificada e l’os ja es remaugut e semblantz ad aquels, lahoras rectifiqua tot aquo am la tua vertut.
If the bandage has loosened and the bone is misaligned, correct it with your skill.

E considera mays si le nutriment es prohibit pervenir al membre per superfluitat de strictura, quar lahoras cove que mollifiques aquel un petit e laysses aquel per alcus dias entro que corra ad aquel le nutriment, e aprop strenh aquel.
Check if the tightness restricts nutrition to the limb; if so, loosen it slightly for a few days to allow nutrition flow, then retighten.

Mays si al malaute no accideys alcuna causa de aquelas que havem ditas, lahoras no cove que sia desliat entro aprop xx dias o enviro de aquels.
If none of these issues occur, do not loosen the bandage for about twenty days.

E aprop sia suspenduda la ma del malaute per la sua vertut de movement agitatius, e fay aquel dormir sobre le sieu dos.
Suspend the patient's hand to encourage movement and have them sleep on their back.

E sapias que aquesta fractura es restaurada en xxx dias o en xxxii dias, o fort leu es restaurada en xxviii dias, e tot aquo es segon la disposicio de las compleccios e las disposicios de la vertut.
Know that this fracture heals in thirty to thirty-two days, or even twenty-eight days, depending on the individual's constitution and vitality.

Capitol .xiii. 
Chapter 13: 

De restauracio de fractura de la pinche de la ma e dels ditz.
On the restoration of fractures of the wrist and fingers.

Sapias que a la pinche de la ma e als nuzes dels ditz tart endeve fractura, e no accideys a lor sino atricio motas veguadas.
Know that fractures of the wrist and knuckles of the fingers are rare, and they usually experience wear and tear.

E quan accideys a la ma fractura o atrissio, lahoras cove que·l malaute segua cayrat e denant lu lies cezent segon equalitat, e aprop pausa la ma de lu sobre aquela extenduda.
When a fracture or wear happens to the hand, the patient should sit squarely and place their hand extended in front of them.

E aprop le ministre extenda les osses trencatz e·l metge engualhe aquels entro que sian congongitz am bona congoncio.
An assistant should extend the broken bones, and the doctor should align them properly.

E lahoras cove que pause emplastre e estopa, si no accideys apostema caut; e aprop pausa stela desus segon la quantitat del loc, e tu ja has envolopada aquela en drap de li.
Then, apply a plaster and cotton if there is no severe abscess, and place a splint according to the injury's location, wrapping it in a cloth.

Mays si la trincadura es en las partidas dedintz deves le ventre de la palma, e lahoras fay semblant de spera de drap, e comanda al malaute que strenha aquela am la sua palma trincada; aprop sia strenguda am drap lonc.
If the fracture is on the inner side of the palm, create a cloth ball and instruct the patient to grasp it with the injured palm, securing it with a long cloth.

E sia la stelha de cuer am drap en le qual sia levitat, per so que le cuer sia aplicat a la palma; e strenh aquela segon que cove.
The splint should be padded with cloth to be gentle on the palm, and tighten it as necessary.

Mays si la fractura es a las partidas defora, lahoras cove que pauses desus stela e autre estela de la partida dejos en la palma, per so que la ma sia uberta e dreyta; e aprop pausa la strictura, ayssi cum es revolvuda la ma a la rateta entre les ditz am liamentz.
If the fracture is on the outer side, place a splint on top and another on the palm side to keep the hand open and straight, and secure it with a bandage wrapped between the fingers.

E si accideys fractura a alcu dels nozes dels ditz, lahoras si es le dit pous, sia engualat segon que cove e aprop sia strenhut am la palma e si·t voles, pausa a lu astela petita dreyta per so que sia elevada la fractura e no sia mauguda.
If a fracture occurs in any of the knuckles, especially the thumb, align and secure it properly with the palm, and if desired, place a small splint to elevate the fracture and prevent movement.

Mays si la fractura es en les autres ditz, ayssi cum en aquel del mieg loc, o en le indic, o en le auricular, o en le anular, lahoras sia engualhat e liat am le dit sa le qual siec aquel; o sian totz liatz segon continuacio, e es milhor; o pausa sobre aquel stela petita, ayssi cum havem dit en le pous.
For fractures in other fingers, like the middle, index, little, or ring finger, align and bind them to the adjacent healthy finger, or bind all together, which is better, or place a small splint as described for the thumb.

E considera, en la tua restauracio, e aprop aquela, la disposicio de apostema caut e oppose — am la tieua operacio — am aquo que cove quan accideys alcuna causa de aquelas, segon que es iterada la narracio de lu.
In the restoration process, consider the possibility of severe abscess and address it appropriately, following the methods previously described.

Capitol .xiv. 
Chapter 14: 

De restauracio de fractura del os de la coyssa.
On the restoration of fractures of the thigh bone.

Le os de la cueyssa motas veguadas es trencat e es declarat al sentiment segon que es convertit a la partida denant e a la pus sobirana.
The thigh bone often breaks and is identified by its misalignment forward and upward.

E la restauracio de lu se fa enayssi que·l liament es strenhut sobre la fractura e autre liament dejos la fractura, e le malaute sia prostrat sobre le sieu ventre e sobre la cara.
Restoration involves tightly bandaging the fracture and another bandage below it, with the patient lying face down.

E aprop le ministre extenda tot le liament a la sua partida segon la qualitat, quan la fractura es en le mieg loc del os.
An assistant should extend the entire bandage according to the injury's nature when the fracture is in the middle of the bone.

Mays si es propdana a la razitz de la cueyssa, lahoras sia le liament propda al denolh a la partida del pentenilh, per so que la extencio caja en sus, e le autre liament dejos la fractura.
If near the hip joint, place the bandage near the knee on the thigh so that the extension is upward, and another bandage below the fracture.

E semblantment si la trencadura es propdana al denolh, lahoras sia fayt le liament propda al denol, e sia la extencio a las partidas dejos.
Similarly, if the fracture is near the knee, place the bandage near the knee and extend it downward.

E aprop le metge enguale le os am amduas las sieuas mas entro que reduzesca aquel segon la semblansa natural e l’os es conjungit per bona conjunccio; lahoras cove que pauses emplastre e strictura, si no accideys al membre apostema.
The doctor should then align the bone with both hands to its natural position and ensure good alignment; then apply a plaster and bandage unless there is an abscess.

Mays si accideys en lu apostema, lahoras tu layssa aquel per alcus dias entro que l’apostema caut sia cedat, e aprop retorna a la tua curacio.
If an abscess occurs, leave it for a few days until it subsides, then return to the treatment.

La strictura de lu sia ayssi fayta: cove que envolopes sobre la fractura una benda dura, e dobla aquella dos o tres veguadas, e remaugua de lu superfluitat; e aprop envolopa la camba entro que pervengua al talo e a la razitz de la cueyssa.
The bandage should be applied firmly, doubled two or three times, and any excess removed; then wrap the leg from the foot to the hip.

E intromet lonc fiel entre la cueyssa e la camba prop del denol a las partidas dejos, e venguan las extremitatz del fiel de la partida pus sobirana de las doas partz, e aprop revolveys sobre la camba e la cueyssa aquo que superflueys de la benda.
Place a long cloth between the thigh and leg near the knee, with the ends reaching the uppermost part of the leg, and wrap any excess cloth around the leg and thigh.

E aprop pausa sobre la cueyssa en le loc de aquela fractura astelhas, e pausa de aquelas una stela sobre le os de la camba.
Place splints over the fracture on the thigh and another splint on the leg bone.

E aprop uempli las vacuitatz entre la camba e la cuoyssa am draps mols, per so que sia coagulada la extrictura.
Fill the gaps between the leg and thigh with soft cloths to ensure firm bandaging.

E aprop comensa am strictura fort del mieg sobre le loc de la fractura am tres envolucios o quatre, e quant mays tu te alonhas am liament del loc de la fractura, la tua strictura sia menor e pus leugiera e pus molha.
Start with a tight bandage in the middle of the fracture with three or four wraps, and as you move away from the fracture site, make the bandage looser and softer.

E aprop exten a doas extremitatz del fiel a las partidas dejos entro que pervengua a la cavilha del pe, e strenh amdoas las extremitatz de las stelhas del autra part per so que·l liament no sia remaugut del sieu loc.
Extend the ends of the cloth to the lower parts, reaching the ankle, and tighten both ends of the splints so the bandage stays in place.

E aprop leyssa la strectura sobre aquel, don esta ayssi que no accideys al membre corrosio ni apostema caut ni emflacio e semblantz ad aquels; e si accideys alcuna causa de aquelas, adonc cueta te am desliament de lu, e rectifica aquo que accideys tot aprop, segon que havem dit motas veguadas.
Leave the bandage as it is, ensuring it doesn't cause corrosion, severe abscess, or swelling; if any such issues arise, quickly remove the bandage and correct the issue as described.

Mays si en le os es pessa del os la qual pongua, lahoras cove que tu engualhes aquel segon que a tu es possibla; e sino, fen sobre lu e remau aquel, e cura am aquo del qual es precedida la rememoracio entro que sia sanat.
If there is a bone fragment, align it as much as possible; if not, remove it and treat it according to previous instructions until healed.

E alcunas veguadas es strenhuda aquesta fractura de la coyssa otra aquo que sian ajustadas a lu stelhas, ayssi cum havem dit en le adjutori e·n le bras.
Sometimes this fracture of the thigh is supported with splints as described for the forearm and arm.

Mays empero en la restauracio de lu en tal manieyra fayta no accideys al malaute claudicacio; e si es restaurada sola, otra aquo que li sia applicada l’autra camba, lahoras es necessari que claudique aquel del qual es tostemps.
In this manner of restoration, the patient does not develop a limp; if restored alone without the other leg's support, the patient will likely limp.

E sapias que la coyssa es strenhuda en xl dias o un pauc mes o un pauc mens, e tot aquo es segon la diversitat de las compleccios e de las autras dispozicios.
Know that the thigh should be bandaged for 40 days, give or take, depending on the patient's constitution and other factors.

De restauracio de la fractura de la rodela del denolh.
On the restoration of fractures of the kneecap.

Sapias que fractura de la rodela del denol tart endeve, mays accideys a lu motas veguadas atrissio.
Know that fractures of the kneecap are rare but often suffer wear and tear.

Mays si accideys a lu fractura, lahoras no es sino fissura o trauc en las suas partidas, e aquo es am plagua o ses plagua, e sobre aquo tot es estat am le sentiment.
If a fracture occurs, it is usually a crack or break in its parts, either with or without a wound, identified by symptoms.

E la restauracio de lu es enayssi que sia engualat aquo que es romput de las partidas de lu am les ditz entro que sia agreguat e conjongit segon que es possible per equacio e facilitat e fabricacio.
Restoration involves aligning the broken parts with the fingers until they are joined as much as possible with proper adjustment and ease.

E aprop considera totas las disposicios las quals havem recomtadas en las autras fracturas, ayssi cum es apostema caut e semblant ad aquels enaissi que se oppause a tot accident am aquo que a lu es convenient entro que sia sanat.
Consider all the conditions described for other fractures, such as severe abscesses, and address any complications appropriately until healed.

Chapter 16. 

De restauracio de la fractura de la camba.
On the restoration of a broken leg.

Sapias que en la camba so dos osses dels quals la un es gros, e es le nompnat per nom de la camba; e l’autra es subtil, e es nompnat focil.
You should know that in the leg there are two bones, one of which is large and is called the leg bone; and the other is thin and is called the fibula.

E accideys a quascus de las specias de fractura aquo que accideys als dos osses del bras, e per aquo es fayta restauracio de lu ayssi cum restauracio del bras engualment, e la operacio de lu es una.
And what happens with each type of fracture also happens to the two bones of the arm, and therefore the restoration is done similarly to the restoration of the arm, and the operation is the same.

E si so trincatz dos osses ensemps, la camba es convertida a totas partidas.
And if both bones are broken together, the leg is turned in all directions.

E si es trinquat le os pus subtil, la camba es convertida a las partidas Denant.
And if the thinner bone is broken, the leg is turned forward.

E si es trincat le os pus gros, atrobas aquel dejos, e es de aquelas causas que no so a tu ameguadas.
And if the thicker bone is broken, you find it below, and it is for reasons that are not hidden from you.

E aprop aministra extencio e equacio e liguacio de las astelas segon aquel engualment.
And then administer extension, alignment, and binding of the splints according to that alignment.

Mays empero cove, si la fractura de la camba es laja havent motas satagias, que la extencio sia mendre e pus leugiera, e alleuja am la tua vertut.
But it is necessary, if the leg fracture is extensive and has many splinters, that the extension is less and lighter, and ease it with your skill.

E en la camba es alcuna causa de operacio sobre le bras, e es quan tu engualas las stelhas e que comples tota la tieua operacio, lahoras tu prendras pessas de fustz de pi le qual es pausat dejos las cauzas las quals so pausades en solies, e so faytas eyssament de brancas de palma; aligeys de aquellas a las quals es petita groceza, e no sia ges de las manudas, e sia la longuesa de aquellas segon la longuesa de la camba, e del denol entro al pus dejos.
And in the leg, there is some operation over the arm, and it is when you align the splints and complete all your operation, then you will take pieces of pine wood which are placed under the things which are usually placed on the ground, and they are made from palm branches; bind those of small thickness, and not those of the smallest ones, and their length should be according to the length of the leg, from the knee to the lowest part.

E aprop envolopa sobre quascuna drap en doas envolucios segon la longitut de lu, e pausa la una sobre la partida de la camba de la una part e l’autra del autra part, e sian del denol entro al pus bas loc del pe.
And then wrap around each cloth in two wrappings according to its length, and place one on one side of the leg and the other on the other side, from the knee to the lowest part of the foot.

E aprop lias las doas stelhas en tres locs de doas extremitatz e al mieg loc, quar am aquesta strectura la camba es prohibida de clinar a la partida dextra e sinistra, e sta per bona stacio.
And then tie the two splints in three places, at both ends and the middle, because with this structure, the leg is prevented from bending to the right or left, and it stays in good position.

E ja es aministrat un brasset de fust segon la longuesa de la camba; e sia pausada en lu la camba per so que conserve aquel de movement.
And a small wooden brace is already administered according to the length of the leg; and the leg is placed in it to prevent movement.

E majorment cove que tu fassas aquo en fractura, e quan am aquela es plagua propriament.
And it is especially necessary that you do this in a fracture, and when with it there is appropriate pain.

E aprop considera en quascun jorn la camba e studia am aquel per derier studi, e tu le guardes de apostema e de imflacio o de autres causas semblantz; e cum accideys alcuna causa de aquelas, lahoras opausa te a lu am aquo que cove entro que sia sanat.
And then examine the leg daily and study it thoroughly, and guard it from abscess and swelling or other similar causes; and if any of these occur, then treat it with what is necessary until it is healed.

De la fractura del talo e dels osses del pe e dels ditz.
On the fracture of the heel and the bones of the foot and the toes.

Al talo no accideys fractura de tot; mays als osses del pe accideys fractura alcunas veguadas; e als ditz del pe pauc accideys fractura, e no accideys a lor sino atricio en las mes de disposicio.
The heel does not suffer fractures often; but the bones of the foot sometimes do; and fractures of the toes are rare, and they usually only suffer from bruising due to their position.

E si als osses del pe endeve fractura e vezes aquels osses esser elevatz sobre si entre lor, lahoras le malaute pause le sieu pe sobre la terra preparat ayssi cum anant.
And if a fracture occurs in the bones of the foot and sometimes these bones are elevated over one another, then the patient should place their foot on the ground as if walking.

E aprop pausa la un pe sobre aquo que es elevat de aquels osses, e aprop calca aquels, e prem, e engualha aquels entro que torno en los locs.
And then place one foot on what is elevated from those bones, and then press, and align them until they return to their places.

And then place a plaster and a compress on top, and place under the arch of the foot a small board with two flat ends.

E aprop strenh aquela am le pe am strectura descent, pus que tu has envolopada aquela am draps e am autres causes de las quals indigeys.
And then secure it to the foot with a decent bandage, after wrapping it with cloth and other necessary things.

E cum a lu passan tres dias o quatre, lahoras tu deslia le liament, quar tu atrobaras les osses engualatz, o sian trincatz o sian dislocatz, e la operacio en aquels es ayssi co coneysses.
And when three or four days have passed, then untie the binding, because you will find the bones aligned, whether they were broken or dislocated, and the operation on them is as you know.

Mays si alcus ditz son trincatz, lahoras restaura aquels, e enguala aquels ayssi cum yeu e recomtat a tu en la restauracio dels ditz de la ma.
But if any toes are broken, then restore them, and align them as I have told you in the restoration of the fingers of the hand.

E aprop pausa al dit trincat stela segon la longitut del dit, e sia pus lada de lu un pauc; e aprop dejos le pe aquesta taula la qual e a tu recomtada, e strenh aquela am strictura decent.
And then place a splint on the broken toe according to the length of the toe, and make it a bit wider; and then under the foot place the board that was recommended to you, and secure it with a decent bandage.

Mays si aquo que es trincat dels osses so dos o tres o mays, lahoras tu pausa sobre quascun dit astela de la sua quantitat envolopada en drap leon, e strenh la taula en le pus bas del pe, e sia stant sobre la un dels caps de la taula foro le ventre del pe per que la tengua am bona retencio.
But if what is broken are two or three or more bones, then place on each toe a splint of its size wrapped in soft cloth, and secure the board to the lower part of the foot, and let one of the ends of the board stand outside the arch of the foot to hold it in good retention.

E es convenient a tu que no oblides que no consideres totas las causas las quals que e ditas a tu en las autras fracturas dels accidentz que havem dit; e opausa te a tot accident am aquo que cove.
And it is necessary for you not to forget to consider all the causes that have been mentioned to you in other fractures of the accidents we have


Capitol .xviii.
Chapter 18.
De fractura del conh de la femna e del os del pentenilh e de la vergua del home.
 On the fracture of the woman's pubic bone and the man's pelvic bone and penis.

Quan le conh de la femna es trincat, lahoras fay aquela ceser en cezela cayrada, e aprop enclina aquela a la partida del dos un petit, e sia tenguda detras.
When the woman's pubic bone is broken, then make her sit in a square seat, and then incline her a little towards the back, and she should be held there.

E aprop la matrona umpla le conh de coto, e sia fayt en le conh de lu ayssi cum spera; e aprop la femna sia concutida, e eleva le dos de lu petit a petit, quar tot aquo es fora-getat entro que sia denant la partida del conh ayssi cum spera e l’os trincat retorna.
And then the midwife fills the pubic area with cotton, and it should be made in the shape of a sphere; and then the woman should be shaken, and raise her back little by little, because all of this is pushed out until the front part of the pubic area is spherical and the broken bone returns.

E aprop pausa pulvils sobre le dos de lu, e quan vol urinar remaugua le coto am facilitat e aprop urine, e reduzeys e retorna aquel segon la manieyra segon la qual mezist aquel al comensament, e aprop retorne al sieu pulvil primier.
And then place powders on her back, and when she wants to urinate, remove the cotton easily and then she urinates, and replace it and return it in the same way you placed it at the beginning, and then return to her original powder.

E fassa ayssi per vii dias o enviro aquels, quar aquel es restaurat.
And do this for seven days or so, because that is the time needed for it to heal.

E si voles, pren una vezica de ovela e strenh sobre le trauc de lu una canula de canavera; e entromet tota la vesica en le conh de lu, e aprop ensuffla en la canula am vertut entro que la vesica sia imflada dedintz le conh, quar la fractura retorna.
And if you wish, take a sheep's bladder and attach to its opening a cane tube; and insert the entire bladder into the pubic area, and then blow into the tube with force until the bladder is inflated within the pubic area, because the fracture will return.

E aprop sia umplida de coto e estia per alcus dias segon que havem recomtat, entro que sia sanat.
And then fill it with cotton and let it stay for a few days as we have said, until it is healed.

E quan le os del pentenil de home o de femna es trincat, lahoras aministra en la restauracio e agulacio de lu aquo que havem recomtat en l’os del anca.
And when the pelvic bone of a man or woman is broken, then administer in the restoration and alignment of it what we have recommended for the hip bone.

E aquo que es dreyt no es occultat en aquestas fracturas proprinquas e que pauc endeveno, majorment ad aquel al qual es alcun studi e us e enten aquest meu libre mot; quar aquela fractura significa a tu en las majors disposicios via dreyturiera en la restauracio e en la strictura de lu, e donc enten be.
And what is right is not hidden in these nearby fractures and which occur infrequently, especially to those who have some study and use and understand this book well; because that fracture shows you in the major dispositions a straight path in the restoration and alignment of it, so understand well.

Mays en la vergua del home quan es trincada, pren guarguamela de auca, e met la vergua en aquella; e aprop pausa sobre lu envolucio de drap, e sia envolopada, e aprop sia layssada per tres dias o enviro aquels, e sia sanada.
But for the man's penis when it is broken, take goose grease, and place the penis in it; and then wrap it with cloth, and it should be bandaged, and then left for three days or so, and it will be healed.

Capitol .xix.
Chapter 19:
De restauracio de fractura dels osses quan es am plagua.
On the restoration of bone fractures with wounds.

Convenient es ad aquel al qual accideys fractura am plagua, e majorment si le os es gran ayssi cum es le os de la cuoyssa o de l’adjutori, o semblant ad aquel, que tu te cuoytes e fleubotomes aquel tantost si las condicios de fleubotomia a tu o testifican ayssi cum desus havem dit.
It is suitable for someone who has a fracture with a wound, especially if the bone is large like the thigh bone or the humerus, or similar, that you act quickly and perform bloodletting immediately if the conditions for bloodletting justify it as we have previously mentioned.

E si la plagua eflueys sanc, lahoras cove que tu te coytes a la retencio de lu enayssi que tu polverizes sobre lu zegi trissat, si a tu autra causa no es present.
And if the wound is bleeding, then you must quickly stop it by sprinkling powdered chalk on it if you have no other remedy available.

E aprop comensa restaurar la fractura en aquel meteys dia, e no prolongues aquo, si no accideys apostema.
And then begin to restore the fracture on the same day, and do not delay this unless an abscess occurs.

Mays si accideys apostema caut, lahoras tu layssa la restauracio de lu entro al ix dia, entro que sia cedat le apostema, e no apropinques a lu en le tertz dia e·l iiii de tot, quar tu faras accidir mals accidentz.
But if an abscess occurs, then delay the restoration until the ninth day, until the abscess subsides, and do not approach it on the third or fourth day at all, as this could cause bad complications.

Mays si le os trencat es eminent sobre la codena descubert, lahoras cove que te perforses reduzir aquel e engualar aquel am las tuas mas am facilitat e am pauca extencio.
But if the broken bone is protruding through the skin, then you must forcibly reduce and align it with your hands gently and with minimal extension.

Mays si extencio no es a tu preparada e la equacio de lu am las tieuas mas, lahoras tu reduzeys aquel am las tuas mas am aquest sturment; e es sturment le qual es fayt de ferr, la longitut del qual es de vii ditz o de viii e la latitut del qual es segon la quantitat de la plagua; e per aquo es necessari al metge que prengua de aquels tres o quatre segon la quantitat que indigeys ad aquo en la curacio en tota specia de fractura.
But if the extension and alignment cannot be done with your hands alone, then reduce it with this instrument; it is an iron tool, seven or eight fingers long and its width according to the size of the wound; and it is necessary for the physician to have three or four of these according to what is needed for the treatment of each type of fracture.

E sia redon, e sia en lu pauca groceza per so que no sia doblat deves la comprecio sobre aquel en la hora de la operacio.
And it should be round and slightly thick so that it does not bend under compression during the operation.

E sia de aguda extremitat al qual sia marge en las sieuas extremitatz; e sia le desus de lu a grossetut tendent, e de la maytat de lu entro a las partidas.
And it should have a sharp end with a margin at the extremities; and its upper part should be of increasing thickness from the middle towards the ends.

E aquesta es la forma de lu:
And this is its form:

E es nompnat en grec “labre volentz atelarem”, so es paleta pauca.
And it is named in Greek “labre volentz atelarem”, which means small spatula.

Per que cove que sia pausada la extremitat de lu acuda elevada sobre la extremitat del os eminent.
So the sharp end should be placed over the protruding end of the bone.

E inpelleys aquel en una veguada entro que retorne le os, e sia engualat am alcuna equacio.
And push it in one movement until the bone returns, and it is aligned properly.

E donc esforsa te engualar las extremitatz de la fractura entre lor, e si la extremitat de lu trencada es subtil, e no pren aquela le sturment per bona axcepcio, lahoras cove que tu inscidas la extremitat de aquel os entro que l’insturment haja poder de aquo.
And then strive to align the fracture ends together, and if the broken end is thin and does not accept the instrument well, then you must incise the end of that bone until the instrument can hold it.

Mays si no podes reduzir le os de tot am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras enscideys aquel am aquo que coveneys a lu dels inscizoris les quals havem ditz; o serra aquel am una de las serras en qualque manieyra sia a tu possible.
But if you cannot reduce the bone completely with what we have recommended, then incise it with a suitable instrument as we have mentioned; or saw it with one of the saws in whatever way is possible for you.

E aprop ratz aquel que roman en le os de asperitat e de scorsas menudas.
And then scrape away the remaining roughness and small scales from the bone.

E cum le os es reduzit, e aprop la reduccio le malaute atroba dolor vehement ledent, lahoras sapias que le os no es retornat al sieu loc natural; e adonc fay aquo quar tu confereyses al malaute gran juvament.
And when the bone is reduced, if the patient experiences severe pain afterwards, then know that the bone has not returned to its natural place; and then do this because you will give the patient great relief.

Cum es complida la tua restauracio la qual fas al os, e lahoras submergeys drap en vi stiptic negre, e propriament si es en estiu, e no pauses sobre la plagua cerot ni autre causa en la qual sia oli, per so que no fassa en lu accidir poyredura e corropcio.
When you have completed the restoration of the bone, then soak a cloth in black astringent wine, especially if it is summer, and do not place a plaster or anything containing oil on the wound, so that it does not cause rot and corruption.

E aprop aministra stelas en la hora del tieu compliment de la restauracio de l’os, e layssa la plagua descuberta enayssi que inscidas le trauc am forfexs e uses de envolucios segon la quantitat de la plagua.
And then apply splints during the completion of the bone restoration, and leave the wound uncovered so that you can make incisions with scissors and use wrappings according to the size of the wound.

E guarda te am tota cautela que no strenhas la plagua am la fractura, quar motas veguadas an fayt aquo les fols metges, e fero accidir sobre les sieus malautes mort o malautia corrodent o zuthement, so es sania.
And be very careful not to tighten the wound with the fracture, as many foolish doctors have done this, causing their patients death or corroding disease or severe inflammation.

E si la tieua strictura leugiera, molli, diversa de la strictura de las autras fracturas.
And let your bandaging be light, soft, and different from the bandaging of other fractures.

E si la plagua es gran o es plagua mala, e temes sobre aquel alcus accidentz mals les quals havem recomtatz, e atrobas dolor en le loc, lahoras no cove que pauses sobre aquel astelas, mays fay ad aquel envolucio de draps durs en loc de stelas e strenh lu am aquelas.
And if the wound is large or a severe wound, and you fear any of the bad complications we have mentioned, and you find pain in the area, then you should not place splints over it, but wrap it with hard cloths instead of splints and secure it with them.

E cum aprop un dia o dos vezes ja la plagua comensar, que en lu sia engendrat brac, lahoras tu osta desus le drap le qual havias pausat sobre aquel am vi, e aprop aministra calguas, enguentz am les quals de nostra constuma es que mediquem las plaguas, ayssi cum enguentz tetrafarmacon e semblantz ad aquel.
And after a day or two when the wound starts to form a scab, then remove the cloth you placed over it with wine, and then apply dressings and ointments with which we usually treat wounds, like tetrapharmacum ointment and similar ones.

E conveneys a tu que deslias le liament e considera la plagua en quascun dia mati e vespre entro que sia consolidada e fermada, e cove que·l membre sia preparat en tal manieyra que la poyredura corra de lu a las partidas dejos am facilitat.
And you must loosen the bandage and examine the wound every day, morning and evening, until it is consolidated and firm, and the limb must be positioned in such a way that any rot drains away from it easily.

Si a la plagua passan motz dias, e no es consolidada ni es abscindit de lu le brac, lahoras sapias que aqui so satagias de las petitas per que cove enquieras la plagua am tenta.
If many days pass and the wound is not consolidated and the scab has not separated from it, then know that there are small fragments which you must search for in the wound with a probe.

E de aquellas satagias aquellas que so separadas remau e extratz, aquellas que de lor no so separadas e pongen le membre e fan accidir dolor, perforsa te a inscidir aquellas segon que a tu aquo es possibla.
And remove and extract those fragments that are separated, and for those that are not separated and are causing pain and inflammation, you must incise them as much as is possible for you.

E si accideys a la plagua zuchem o eluchen, so es stiomenios, o autra specia de corrupcio e de putrefaccio, lahoras cove que pauses a quada un de aquels am aquo que conveneys a lu de la curacio del qual es precedida narracio en le sieu capitol.
And if the wound develops pus or discharge, such as abscesses, or any other type of corruption and putrefaction, then you must treat each of them with the appropriate remedies whose treatment has been previously described in its chapter.

E de aquo en le qual cove que stia lo mieu sermo e tu fassas present la tua pessa: quan os gros es trincat, emineys sobre le membre ayssi cum le os de la coyssa e del ajutori e semblantz ad aquels dels membres grans, e que no presumas atraccio de lu, ni la extraccio de lu quar motas veguadas accideys per aquo la mort; habantz layssa aquel entro que poyresca, quar fort leu cayra per si aprop xx dias o .xxx.;
And this is where my discourse must stay and you present your practice: when a large bone is broken, protruding over the limb like the thigh bone or the humerus and similar large limb bones, do not presume to pull or extract it because this often causes death; instead, leave it until it decays, as it will likely fall off by itself in around 20 or 30 days;

e lahoras cura la plagua si a tu es vist, e si no layssa aquela.
and then treat the wound if you see fit, and if not, leave it alone.

Capitol .xx.
Chapter 20:
De la curacio de nodacio que accideys en le vestigi de alcuna fractura.
On the treatment of swelling that occurs at the site of a fracture.
